# xml 


```python
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET
tree = ET.parse("15CC05180227110215121012_0x0_0x1.xml")
```


```python
root = tree.getroot()
```


```python
root.tag
```




    'annotation'




```python
for child in root : 
    if child.tag == 'object':
        for ob in child:
            print(ob.tag,ob.text)
            if ob.tag == 'bndbox':
                for i in ob:
                    print(i.tag,i.text)
```

    ('name', 'yinlie')
    ('pose', 'Unspecified')
    ('truncated', '0')
    ('difficult', '0')
    ('bndbox', '\n\t\t\t')
    ('xmin', '180')
    ('ymin', '131')
    ('xmax', '366')
    ('ymax', '184')

# xml

from lxml import etree
f = open("15CC05180227110215121012_0x0_0x1.xml")
f = f.read()
root = etree.fromstring(f)
print(etree.tostring(root))

img = np.array(Image.open('000000061471.jpg'))
